name:2â€3â€hâ€hâ€bâ€jâ€hâ€aâ€n
info:International Superior King Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:9 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted February 19, 2024
msg:It's not that the International Hotel is bad, but that Holiday Inn gives too much (Chengde)

The hotel has been opened for more than a year, and the hardware facilities should be the best in the local area [proud]
Swimming pool, gym, spa, restaurant are all available. Staying will get two spa tickets worth 59 (Rehe Spa), which are large in scale and new in facilities. Bathing, sauna, sweat steaming, soaking pool, daily chemicals, bath towels, lounge, children's playground are all available. Except for the lack of gym facilities, there is nothing to complain about.
The service is also in line with the five-star positioning, especially the breakfast restaurant. Although there are a lot of people on holidays, the details are still well controlled. For example, in the area where noodles are cooked, because the noodle soup is hot, there are waiters who will take the initiative to ask if you need help to deliver the food. Usually, if you ask for some items in the room, the robot will deliver them as soon as possible.
Let's talk about breakfast. This is a bit polarized. There are many types and good services, but the taste of the dishes is really average [covering face]
Finally, let's talk about the room. The hotel is divided into two buildings, one is Holiday Inn and the other is International Hotel, but they are connected through the lobby on the first floor. The price of Holiday is normally over 300 including breakfast for two, while International is nearly 500. What is the difference of this nearly 200 price difference? In fact, there are only differences in orientation, decoration style, and smart appliances: specifically, International faces Wulie River, while Holiday faces the bus station (but you can also see Wulie River from the side); the decoration style of International is more business-oriented and the king-size bed room has a bathtub, while Holiday is more casual and has no bathtub; International has electric curtains and smart toilets, while Holiday does not. In addition, all other public facilities including breakfast, swimming pool, and free spa tickets are no different. Whether it is worth it depends on personal preference [proud]
Personally, I think the price-performance ratio of Holiday is over 300, and the price-performance ratio of International is only average, of course, except for the rich [grin] See the pictures for details, the last four are for Holiday.
